# ACORD Template AcroForm Field Inventory

## Overview

Comprehensive inventory of AcroForm fields across 7 ACORD insurance templates. These are interactive PDF forms with fillable fields organized hierarchically by semantic section (NamedInsured, Producer, Policy, etc.). Total fields: **3,120** across **661 checkboxes** and **2,459 text fields**.

## 131 Excess-Umbrella Section 2017-11.pdf — 392 fields, 6 pages

### Page 1 (152 fields)
